He shattered the urn against the earth, and the remains of what was once his love now belonged to the wind, swirling slowly, liberated in a gorgeous sky.

The limousine door opened.  Hank entered and sat beside Kane.  No words were spoken.  Johnny-John drove to the airport.

Kane:  Where was Udders?

Hank:  What?

Kane:  Udders, our manager.

Hank:  Oh.  I fired him.

Kane:  Udders was with us from the beginning- how could you fire him?

Hank:  I was tired of always seeing his nipples through his shirt.

Kane:  Oh.

Hank:  I guess it's like you always say- the more practical clothes are, the dumber they look.

Kane (laughing):  What's so practical about an eye-patch and a jester's hat?

Hank:  See, you get it Kane.  No one else in the entire fucking globe gets it except you.  Everyone says I have a gift.  They say that I have to use it to give something lasting to humanity.  Fuck humanity!  You busted your ass to make Scoundrels performances the most spectacular shows of all time, but I was never performing.  I just acted naturally, and people took me for a show.  You were the only one who ever understood that.  I miss creating with you, man.

Kane:  I miss it too.

Hank:  If I'm meant to bring the fire, then I'll bring the fucking fire- but let's create some wild shit while we're together.

Kane:  We've captured an audience, Easton, and for some reason we have an influence over people.  Let's exact that power for good.  I say we stop trying to outdo one another and just work together.

Hank:  Since when are you so righteous?

Kane:  I've changed.

Hank:  You know, I don't believe in righteousness.  And because I don't believe in righteousness, I don't believe in sin.  Righteousness, Sin, Justice, Liberty, Peace- it's all just fancy wording to me.  But I've come to believe in being.  And because I believe in being, I'll help you.  Because every man has a right to be.

Johnny-John pulled into the airport.

Hank:  Just tell me where the hell we're going.

Kane:  There's this woman I thought you'd like to meet.

Hank:  If she's a woman, as you say, then yes I'd like to meet her.

Kane:  I don't know where she is, but I'm told she's an immortal prostitute.

Hank:  An immortal hooker!

Kane:  That's what I hear.

Hank:  If you're jerking me off, it's not cool.

Kane:  She's supposed to be around two thousand years old by now.

Hank:  We've gotta find this girl.

Kane:  Yeah, I'd like to talk to her.

Hank:  Talk?  You'd like to talk to her?  This chick has done filthier things than a pedophile in a daycare and all you wanna do is talk to her?

Kane:  I've learned a lot about women, Easton.

Hank:  Who knows more about women than me?  I can tell you if she'll swallow the seed before she ever even opens her mouth to say hello.

Kane:  I've been dreaming up a poem about this woman.

The sun stayed at its zenith, directly above the limousine, as if the earth had frozen to center all sunlight directly onto Kane.  The limo stopped before a private jet.  Johnny-John opened the door.

Johnny-John:  Mr. Israele, your plane is waiting.

Hank, Kane, and Apollo boarded the plane, having no idea where they were headed.  Their destination was never important because at that moment, a broad smile stretched the width of Jake Israele's face.  No matter what fate lies in wait, the lighted portrait of Jake Israele will always read WE SHALL WRITE across his forehead, and he will carry this message forever.  Thus, he smiles paradise.

There was a moment when Kane Hailand was God.  Whether you believe God is a being, an idea, an ideal, or even if you believe God is the devil, you must admit that the conception of God is all-powerful only in the realm in which he presides.  God does not see Himself as a god- in his own self-perception, God is a frustrated Artist, penning the terrestrial drama.  What can we say about God as a storyteller if his characters were to never grow or progress?  What sort of Artist would he be?  Surely the Supreme Dramatist applies progress to his narrative.  Since the beginning, we have asked ourselves what portion of God's story results from our will, and what portion from God's direction?  The answer, ultimately, is unimportant.  The story will be written, whether by God or by us.  But God depends on our active participation so that his story may be written- They are no more powerful than You or He or She or I, but WE are more powerful than any force this life can see.  The important thing is that WE characters progress.  All the men who have lived and died and copulated and felt the same vivacity that WE feel now, the same sense of promise and the same divine beckon- WE are the mark of progress.  It is not our duty to think of our many brothers and sanction ourselves as beings of ultimate inconsequence- let this be our inspiration to thrive in our shared responsibility.  Hank Adaline and Kane Hailand created peace.  This is the story we know.  But when the final dawn awakens for humanity to see its dying day, when the rubble is cleared by a blazing wave of fire and light in a lovely apocalypse, and the progenies sift through relics from the lonely race of man, what will their histories have to say in regards to the quest of Heart of the People?  This story, my brothers, WE SHALL WRITE.


* * *

As he is whole, will accept his soul
Is the SOTU.  The train, it never
Stops, though it slows.  It endeavors
Faster than your feet move beneath you.
Follow the tracks.  They will take you to
The only place they know to go.  No
One says a word.  They look at you so
Closely it's as if you don't exist.
You are the reason the train persists.
Tunnel through the gold molten magma,
Beneath the land on heat skates of the
Champion fire.  Chug and rattle Train
Of Power, impervious to bane.
You may never stop and the rail may
Never end, so grip the steel and say
To yourself that no one's ever gripped
Steel before.  The train slows.  Having shipped
Its passengers forever, it will
Only regain speed.  The humble trill
Will never stop, and well, it can't cause
All you know is the train and its buzz.
Still it slows, and the shadows are now
Figurine and familiar somehow.
Listen to the train's seismic rumble
As it stops.  Kindred, as an umbel,
Come Home to mother soil.  The train doors
Part, and draft a cool breeze that is yours.
You fight to exit the train.  You can't
Remember what you fight for, O plant,
But once fighting why stop.  You stumble.
The conductor calls a name.  Jumbled
In an alien tongue, he says that
It is yours.  Is it that you have flat
Forgotten your name in this distant
Dream.  The conductor is insistent.
This is where you get off.  Staring death
In the face of the Jester, your breath
Draws heavy.  Surely your time has come.
Look into the Jester's one eye.  Numb,
You shake his hand.  The fighting expires.
Blow their minds out in a train, inspire
The crowd of people who stand and stare.
Confused and physically impaired,
The crowd of people follow you to
Freedom.   You were once a pharaoh.  You
Were once a beggar.  You were once a
Victor.  Among this crowd You will stay
A Man, and Man be proud- carrying
Your badge of flesh.  You are marrying
The World.  The People wander sunward.
You just have to look.  Feel it leave, Bird,
Feel it go- a steaming slithering
Worm on skates of fire, the lost
Premiere locomotive.  Gone the frost
As it rushes by cart by cart by
Cart until the whistle fades to die.
But You can't shake the Jester's image,
Stroking his glass pelican- barrage
Of birth.  You've seen His face before, but
Nobody is really sure if what
They see is His face.  And somewhere
Hank Adaline and Kane Hailand share
A blithe handshake on a record called
THE TRUTH.  You have been pleasantly mauled.
It has been an exhausting trip on
The Train of Power.  You, now the Sun.
You, now the morning Moon.  Faith come near,
My weary traveler, Touch Me.  Hear
The laughter of the crowd.  People are
Good.  Those who are not Good are as far
From good as their discontent.  They
Desire to be Good, and this ray
Of desire, this recognition that
Good is Good is merely practice at
Evil.  Rustic coils of the gentlest
Beauty lead Neptune's blue ocean mist
To the open sky.  To and fro swings
The land under the feet of the kings
Who have triumphed.  You, the Sleeping Sand,
The Silent Cloud, the Cherished Laughs, and
The two Lovers in endless embrace
Are instruments of the same song.  Pace,
Dancers of the Holy Rhythm, Dance
And Dance and Dance.  Annihilate chance
As the stone erodes beneath you.  There
Is no pressure to conform when fair
Standards are the natural.  You are
One kind- through the measure, through the bar,
Through the canto, through the chorus, You
Are One.  You have variances to
Dazzle, not bewilder you.  You'll find
No difference in your laughter.  Mind
Is neither yours nor mine, it is Ours.
The largest of empires lasts mere hours.
This is a nation of soul- of WE.
Dancing in a Corcle, Dancing, Free.
Bollocks to intercultural war.
There is no merit in the word more,
No merit in the idea of
Separate peoples, for you must Love
As you are Brothers in a blessed
Corcle.  The Corcle is not a test.
It is continuous.  It is whole.
No beginning, no end.  It is full.
WE- the SOTU.  Arise.  Still higher.
Lonely souls sing to Unite.  Choir
Rise together, lonely nevermore.
It is your duty to inspire, your
Fortune to endow your Brother with
The ability to be the myth,
To live the role only you can fill,
To tend to the children in the hill.
Everyone is pregnant, a new life
Harvesting inside you all.  World rife
With beauty, a great garden with two
Gardeners.  This is not to eschew
The self.  This is not a surrender
Of self.  This is the sacred splendor,
Graduation of the self into
What once was.  Sing with might.  All of you.
Mankind is a persisting chorus
And it only sings its song for Us.
Having read the Book, you can trace all
Man to a single act of Love.  Call
To Her- Life, Love, is a gift. All you
Need is Love.  Yes, believe the world to
Be wonderful.  Every grain of Sand,
Every Boy and Girl, every Smile and
Every Tear, is Wonderful.  You reach
Through Her eyes and say not a word.  Speech,
As you say, is meaningless.  Wearing
A white dress, She catches you staring.
She has been a harbor to abuse,
A land mother to hope, to excuse
And prosperity.  A faint scar mars
Her uncovered thigh.  It is a scar
That could have only come from living.
Only present for just a giving
Instant and then it's gone, but just
The presence of an instant will thrust
Its presence to eternity.  Sea
Shell eyes, windy smile, prairie belly,
And appalachian breast.  All the world
Sings a song of Love for Her.  Hair curled
In red tresses from the sun and Moon.
She holds a flower pot.  Calls you.  Boon
Of Love.  Ocean child.  Calls you.  Calls you
Into the Beyond, your fingers through
Her hair of floating sky, shimmering
In the ripe golden sun.  Glimmering
Seraph- she'd Love to turn you on.  Plant
Her stunning blossomed Violets, grant
Them to the Earth.  What was once a seed
Is now a will to Live, breathe, and bleed
The SELF OF THE UNIVERSE.  Nestle
Them into the great breathing vessel
Of Our Earth.  She hands you a flower
And Her touch is a kiss, the power
Of Love pulsing in your hand and it
Says what all language amounts to.  Sit
With Her.  Fit with Her.  Love Her garden.
Bathe in Love, all secrets imparted.
Listen to the stars, far behind you
Now.  This is devolution in true
Faith.  Behold!  She sees.  Offering Her
Peace.  Fly beyond the light together,
She will be your guide.  And you sayeth
Unto Her, unto Us, from the pith
Of the SOTU- I will never leave
Your side, You have raised me to believe.


# # #
